Unexpectedly, the five-star hotel experience was great. , arrived at Anyu, the Internet celebrity B&B booked for two nights on the last leg of the journey, with high expectations. But after I came here, I regretted why I didn‚Äôt book a few more nights with five stars. I gave the only negative review (only for the construction of the B&B, and I was very satisfied with the housekeeper and manager). The following reviews can all be verified. I hope it can help. to everyone.
Service: The hotel's service awareness and attitude are great. There is a dedicated butler service. Although the professional level of handling some things is still inferior to that of star hotels, they are all very positive in solving problems. If we hadn't been told about the turndown service, we would have expected less. Turndown service: ÔºúHelp tidy up the clothes and bedding, and then put a card on it saying they can provide eye masks, good night milk, etc. If we need it, we can ask the housekeeper for it. The flip-flops are provided. If you feel uncomfortable, you can ask the housekeeper to exchange them for disposable cotton slippers> I wonder if we can put the disposable items provided directly in the room instead of asking the housekeeper to ask for them again.
Travel photography experience: The hotel reservations were marked as free travel photography. When we were doing the guide in November, we called and asked if booking for two nights meant two travel photography. The phone said it was like this, so we booked it. Two nights. (To be fair, the price is the same every night, and there are no discounts for consecutive bookings. You should also enjoy the same benefits every day). The day before we checked in, when the housekeeper added WeChat, we asked by the way to confirm this matter. At this time, the housekeeper told us that it depends on the guests staying, and each customer will receive a travel photo no matter how many days they stay. At this time, I told me that I had called to ask about this in November, and the housekeeper said that maybe my colleagues had made a mistake. Normally, they only have one copy of the travel photo shoot, but they could help us apply for an extra copy. However, I still think this is the right we deserve. The housekeeper also reminded us that it is not normally available, but will give us more, which does not sound very comfortable. But it can be regarded as a positive solution to the problem. Travel Photography is a cooperative agency, and the photographer who came here took about ten minutes to complete the photo. The photo was quite poor, and we didn‚Äôt want to refine it. Don‚Äôt expect the free photography.
Meals: Breakfast and afternoon tea are the highlights of the hotel. The quality and service are basically better than other B&Bs, and they are very good. The service was very good during the meal. I ordered coconut chicken hot pot for dinner, but it didn‚Äôt suit the taste and I ate half of it because I was afraid of wasting it.
The key points are the hotel's environment and facilities.
Room: Rooms priced at 1,500 yuan have no windows and are extremely small (this size cannot accommodate a bathtub, and there is no place to dry underwear and socks). There is only one completely transparent door on the side (the house is probably a container with a door), so when you go to the room to rest, you have to draw the curtains for privacy. The whole room is dark, and you can't open the curtains even if you get up early in the morning. To let the sunlight in, you can only wait until you finish washing and dressing before opening the door curtains. The room was just a place to sleep. It was too small and had no light, so it was very stuffy. The sound insulation is super, super, super bad, there is no sound insulation at all! The sound of the faucet running next door would wake us up at seven o'clock in the morning. We are not light sleepers at all. We were very angry about this. We really didn't want to make do with it when we were on vacation, so we applied to the housekeeper to cancel the room for the next day. I really don‚Äôt understand why this kind of room that is full of surprises is hung on the platform for sale and affects everyone‚Äôs holiday mood. Regarding the sound of the faucet, the store owner said that this has never happened before and that he would have to go to the engineering depar**ent to investigate and verify. A certain book complained about soundproofing. After so many years of driving, I don‚Äôt know how to soundproof my room. Why are I just checking now? We were unlucky to meet the guy next door who was washing on top of us at seven o'clock and was startled to wake us up.
Regarding check-out: I was very angry after being woken up at 7 o'clock in the morning. I contacted the housekeeper immediately. The housekeeper agreed to cancel the room for the second night and apologized. But the plan they proposed was to "refund the room for two days, and then I would pay the first day's room at a discounted price." The reason was that "their backend couldn't refund one day alone." I don't know if they were lying or not. I really won't be refunding it. I could apply for a one-day refund on Ctrip alone, but the housekeeper said that he would help ** handle the check-out. He took his mobile phone to help ** handle the check-out and directly applied for a full refund for two days. After I found out, he said I don't accept this. I only accept a one-day refund. I need an order from Ctrip to guarantee my rights. The housekeeper then said that he would have to wait until the manager went to work before he would be able to help me handle it. Then we continued to choose alternative hotels, and waited until after nine o'clock when the duty manager came to work and contacted us. The attitude was very good, they reassured us throughout the whole process and promised to check out. However, their backend may be because the housekeeper used my mobile phone to apply for a two-day check-out but the processing timed out. Their backend was no longer able to refund me for only one day. At this time, I chose Ctrip customer service to intervene. Ctrip adheres to the principle of customer first, which is very good. It took a while to resolve the subsequent matters smoothly. The two managers on duty at the B&B at the back dealt with the problem very professionally. They kept negotiating with us about the process and feelings, and kept apologizing to appease our emotions. The manager at the back even planned to send us a lunch to express his apology, but we were not very hungry. There was no need, and seeing that we loved dragon fruit, he offered to mail some home for us. I got a souvenir after leaving the store. It can be said that the hotel's service restored the mood affected by the accommodation conditions.
Facilities: hair dryer, Dyson, and toiletries should be good too; the room has no big lights and is rather dim, which makes it feel particularly dull with no windows. It's difficult to put on makeup in the room, it's too small, and it's uncomfortable to use the makeup mirror half-crouched. It is impossible to watch TV without a membership. I asked the housekeeper, and the housekeeper said that you need to sign up as a member to watch it. Maybe my expectations were a little high. Because there are many hotels near Haitang Bay, there is a duty-free city around, and the transportation is very convenient. In comparison, the location here is relatively remote, and many local drivers do not know that there is a hotel here. But it really feels like a paradise, a paradise here. Figure 2 is the first perspective of driving to Anyu, which is very beautiful.

Although the entire hotel is small, it is full of details; every clerk is very gentle and patient, and the WeChat reply is very fast. The hotel has 24-hour online staff, fresh fruit available around the clock (free of charge, coconuts are charged separately), afternoon tea with a wide range of categories from 2:00 to 4:00, good night milk, and free charging treasure. If you are hungry, you can also ask for sandwiches, buns and the like. All in all, the service is impeccable, and I even feel that only the guests can't think of it, and Anyu can't do it.

Anyu's privacy is also very good. Guests who don't live in the store can't eat here. Whether it's stir-fried vegetables or coconut chicken hot pot, it tastes great. Personally, I think stir-fried vegetables and seafood are even better.

In short, this place is very suitable for young couples or people who prefer quietness and peace. To be honest, it is not very suitable for bringing children, because compared with hotels such as Edition and Crown, there are basically no entertainment facilities and activities for children. In addition, if you don't want to lie down in the hotel, stroll by the sea, or want to visit more scenic spots, it is not suitable for this place, because there are indeed some restrictions on transportation and location.

An Yu is very aware of her strengths and weaknesses, so she pays great attention to details such as service and hotel decoration, and there are services such as free delivery to the airport.

Everyone thinks clearly about their own needs. If you have high service requirements and don‚Äôt like to visit scenic spots, people who like quietness will definitely like this place.
